Comment: jenhatzung said "Today's @shepercolates #coffeedatewithSP topic is loneliness. This is something I've struggled with in my early 20s and again last year when Scott deployed. I love getting a bit of alone time to recharge my batteries but when I spend too much time alone I think too much. I start to question myself and over analyze everything. I think in my early 20s it was because I wasn't sure who I was and I needed to be around people to feel like I belonged. I needed validation. In my 30s I've really tried to embraced the idea that I need to just be me, I need to be comfortable in my own skin and be proud of who I am. I think that is what I boils down to, being proud of who you are. Loneliness during deployment is a whole different beast. @daniellespurge and I will be talking more in depth about loneliness in this Friday's #shepercolates episode."
